申報本埠增刊談言蓄婢制度是應該廢除的  吹　　前日增刋中發表了夢若君「廢婢運動」一文，鄙人一時心血來潮，便做了一篇「返廢婢運動」，原是游戲性質，不過於文字之間，太覺肯定，太覺老實，不免搪突了夢若君一些，因此夢若君，又做了一篇「蓄婢制度是不應廢除麼？」夢若君再拿這種官話打來，圖人只有負荊請罪，尙有何說。　　因爲夢若君主張廢婢運動，若拿大義來講，是無可否認的，若以現在情形來講，是絕不可能的，就是夢若亦自認「爲不免失之過早」故鄙人反對廢婢運動，夢若君亦相當的承認，旣經過早，便不能實行，旣經不能實行，非「打官話」而何？因爲打官話的事件，自民國以來；不知聽見了多少，所以我一聽見「打官話」，便要頭痛，現在我們所需要的是實利，所應講的是事實，空頭話可不必談。　　夢若君又說，「蓄婢是一種奴隸制度，又是一種人身買賣行爲，在人類文明進於相當程度的今日，已沒有存在的理由」夢若君拿好大的帽子套在鄙人的頭上，假使打了我一百廿下嘴巴，還是他有道理，不信，請看現在世界怪傑墨索里尼，他爲什麼要出兵征討阿比西尼亞？因爲阿國還有奴隸制度存在，奴隸是一種極野蠻國的行爲，所以墨索里尼不惜犧牲幾萬萬的國幣，出發百餘萬的軍隊，去改造阿國的文明，廢除他們奴隸制度，奴隸制度的禍根，有這樣的厲害，我對於夢若君尙敢說什麽話？只有自己供招，日「蓄婢制度是應該廢除的」　　但是我還有一句話要說明，夢若君謂「女子不幸爲人婢女，常將一生斷送在牛馬奴隸的生活中」，這句話我却絕對不相信，因爲我國蓄婢之制，並不是像菲洲的黑奴一樣，我國蓄婢制度中，（我姑且承認爲制度）有兩種性質，一是臨時的，一是永久的，臨時的曰押，永久的曰賣，押是有時效的，或五六年，或七八年，賣是絕賣，沒有時效的，但是名雖絕賣，婢女服務到相當年齡，（大約在二十歲左右）主人便將該婢遣嫁，從來沒有看見過斷送終身的婢女，並且買賣婢女，爲避免刑事上責任起見，往往寫成過寄的形式，並不算爲買賈，故此種制度，認爲買賣可，認爲非買賣亦可。　　我把上述的事實，旣經說明，我還有兩件事要寫給夢若君一聽，並請讀者一聽，聞現在陝甘等處，民窮財盡，羅掘俱窮，竟將女子出賣，其年齡在二十歲以下的僅賣二十元，若年齡在二十歲以上，則十餘元或七入元不等，凡得脫手（卽賣去）的尙稱爲幸事，其不能賣去，往往竟至飢餓而死，更爲可憐，還有某地，尙有所謂典生子的制度，凡有妻而不能自養，往往典質於人，或沒有妻室，而又不能娶妻者，得向有妻室者租賃若干年，名曰典生子，期滿後或得展期，或聽憑取贖，桑視雙方的感情和經濟情形而定，此種制度，還要比蓄婢制度更爲惡劣，因爲該地經濟的生活情形，萬分困難，無法取締，這當然談不到法律和正義也。　　總之，廢婢運動誠然無可反對，但先要替婢女的生活及婢女父母的生活解决了，再來議這問題，未爲晚也。木屋新居  辛爾　　東京，是太遼闊了。我只約莫知道我這住處的一區，，在東京市內，是不挺繁華，也不極冷落，算作平庸的。大槪有點像上海北四川路那樣吧。　　聽着屋頂上如風吼的高架電車的疾馳聲，行過馬塲驛，沿馬路邊拐，已經處處可見每個轉角處，是幽靜的小石路，默默的伸進去；兩旁盡是悠然柔垂的綠葉，樹枝葉下，半掩半漏的露出石地

Page 16

上的木屋，門前懸着不明不暗的燈，多半是下宿館或者是住家。門邊總是傍樹，有籬有石，剛才走過艷熱交流的繁華的街頭，一下子便轉入殆如村莊的去處，淸靜幽秀，氣息悠柔，使人淸醒。　　如果稍過數百步，望前面，是寬長的大馬路，汽車如流星，街的夜光炫人。我便慣常的發見左側有個大空隙，而怡然轉身。面前變成一帶斜坡，左側臨馬路，一列土堆之上，樹林密密列過，望之蔚然。右側高樹約二十多，幽曠秀壯，盡頭處是一派樹林裏，雜着精巧的木屋，樓窗在燈光下半隱半露。從正面直上斜坡，地上靑草萋萋，是一大曠塲，有如山野間。幾陣淸新的空氣沁人，氣味又有不同，站住甜息，每自開懷而樂，像登臨高峯，領略美景。和白熱化的東京的大都會，簡直如隔一世呢。誰想到便是身置東京市內！　　再行盡曠處，樹林，竹籬，淡淡的燈交映下，隱約現出小巷，我便輕輕的，沒入這裏面去了。　　除了木展踏着沙十的低音外，簡直全無聲息，只像挨過樹葉下，微風吹過，瑟瑟如密語，惹人悠思。但叢林間竹籬內，盡居處，景緻幽秀淸靜無足怪，人衆而能如此，頗可喜可奇。而卽使白天，也無兩樣。　　我記得淸楚，悄悄的行盡二條籬巷，捐個灣，一直斜進深處，有些迷離之槪，那怕是淸謐鮮甜得醉人吧。數顆樹略高出密林，綠葉映黑瓦，至此我總愛凝住而望，心裏輕微的笑，這便是我這飄亡異國的孤獨者的「家」啊！有時彷彿如夢呢。閉上眼都淸晰如畫。略高密林的數顆樹的最後一顆特別濃蔭的樹葉下，露出約莫一個住室的半壁，這恰好是面東，木屋的壁盡是窗，玻璃略啟，愈顯木屋的精巧；殆像幽塔小窗。是這座下宿家的樓上東南面的轉角的一間小住室，我便睡在那上面。　　於是，移步踏着石階，輕輕推開玻璃門，再關上，把布簾也揭過。裏面便有下女探出頭來，俯了幾個像要跪下去的叩頭，婉然吒出兩句通常的客氣話。這是所謂挺有禮貌的日本人經常的習慣。脫鞋後再跨上木板；入室肅然，自己踏着雖久遠而猶潔凈的地板，也須輕輕的呢。這是普通的公寓啊。比故國的公寓直有天淵別。繞各個房間前經過，只能從有沒有燈，辨別出有沒有人住。幽靜得如在深林，無論朝暮午。房間面前是天井，植滿花木，有小水池。上樓，推開沒有可關鎖門的竹窗糊上潔白的紙的房門，脫拖鞋而入。地上是蘆，沒有睡床的。南面也是玻璃窗爲　。一小寫字台靠窗，一隻椅子，寫讀時用的，平常　地而坐。東南面窗外是空隙樹林，隔層木板，便是他家。室之西，是隔一板與鄰室共；但我住將月，不知有無住人，日夜靜無聲息。除從窗上見他家相向的窗內有人外，我似乎不知自己這　住滿了人的木屋是住了許多人。夜來因隔間老鼠通夜遊，頗擾人，便以爲隔壁無人住，詢之主人，痛壁竟居一人呢。日本人是習慣於靜的。小房內還有畫壁，配合起來，直不像住宅，而如櫥中的藝術品。整個房子盡是木造的；但却很堅固，可支持二三十年以上者，這未免有點異。木屋竟如此耐經風雨之吹打。常散步附近，及遼遠的友人處，都是同樣情景，不料都市之冶艷火熱，猶有這樣的處處淸幽秀潔。如同少林佳村的所在。我便挺愛這點，在這遼闊的東京市內。因作木屋前居以記。燈  胡慰雄　　小病了幾天，覺得燈火之可愛了。上海是稱爲不夜城的，黃昏初上，街頭炬通明，照耀如白畫，失去了夜的神　。我寗願住到僻靜的角落角里來，就是了那些明亮的電炬太使眼睛不舒服。晚上應該有一個晶瑩的月亮，閃閃的星光，你把屎子里燈火熄了，獨自憑着窗欄，極目四望，讓寂寞佔有了空間。月亮出沒於雲層之間，你會注視着她面目不稍瞬，恐怕她要逃去似的。或許你心中惦念着某一個人，或某一件事，吳剛伐桂就會從月球里逃出來，而雲層之間是你勝利的戰塲，那個人，那件事，都如你平時有腦海中盤旋般地如約而來；你手臂下的窗欄同時亦像輕氣球似的浮升起來，做夢那樣地你和惦　的那個人，那件事合而爲一。等到你驚醒回來的時候，院子里階前的月光已移上花牆，紫籐花如蟒蛇似的攀附在牆上，虫聲像一曲柔和的催眠歌，你感到輕微的睡意，和衣睡到床上，一個同樣的夢境會追隨着你。　　這是我向來的偏見。但在此次病中我感到；如白晝一般的電炬雖然使眼睛不舒服，一盞昏黃的燈光有時却倍覺可親。　　爲生活所迫，終日周旋於人與人之間，縱然有幾個親熱的朋友，但在某種塲合之中，逼不得已運用處世藝術的手腕來應付對方時，我的心彷彿被毒蛇嚙咬着一樣痛苦。所謂做人，難道必要帶假面具做護身符吧？我時常責問自己，但是自己是沒有方法來答覆這個問題的；因爲我不能不周旋於人與人之間，而假面具還是要牠擋一陣子的。一到生病，是一點起碼的小病，我又覺太孤獨了。我希望有一個或是一羣朋友來看我，自然不奢望他們能够給我一些什麽安慰，大家套起假面具來胡扯一陣也是好的。病中的生活不能像着月亮那樣地詩意化，獨自悠然自得地不覺冷露凝翠袖的。但是沒有一個人來，一只將死的叫哥哥啞而且沙的不時打破寂寞的空間。於是一盞不甚明亮的燈火是我唯一的安慰者了。她底慈母一樣的銀絲光照着我的眠床，照着我的微微炙手的額，我如睡在柔波之上，在搖籃之中；病中的苦痛，寂寞的憤恨，像水沫似的消逝了。我幾乎每天希望夜早一點來，有時扭亮了燈火等着暮色從窗上集合。於是我想起了一個燈的故事。　　是大表姊出閣的那年，我在舅父家吃喜酒，有一個和我同樣年齡的孩患了天花，母親命當夜返家。從舅父家到我家里有十多里路，一個僕人負着我走。是臘月下旬，沒有月亮，提了一盞馬提燈走夜路，我從來沒有這種經騐。我伏在僕人的背上，埋緊頭，目光不敢向四周窺視，那風聲，脚步聲，彷彿鬼嘯似的跟在背後，我祇希望快一點到家。但在半路上我忽然注視着前面的馬提燈來，牠照着我們行動的尺寬地位，　人的兩條腿在黯淡而混暈的燈光中行動，高低不平的路面，是活動的背景，我自高臨下，平凡的路面在優光中剎那間消逝，都變成了奇觀的景物。一路到家，我的視綫沒有離開彙圓的燈光片刻。之後我到縣城讀書，回家時總喜歡走夜路，燈提在自己手中，脚步放慢加快都會發見不同的奇觀。但到都市中來，那些照耀如白畫的電炬我的眼睛受不慣，我喜歡孤獨地憑欄賞月，這或許是到了中年的關係吧？此次小病，使我重行愛好燈火，也是值得紀念的。舅舅  白羽　　　　在輸船上把　冬瓜多嘔了出來的佳福舅舅，坐上了黃包車，迎面吹來帶有姻味的風，身子一陣哆嘈，頭腦子却淸醒多哪！　　這時，佳福舅舅才覺得他的身邊轟立着那高高的屋子，想抬起頭來瞧瞧屋頂倒底是怎麼一個樣兒時，一頂破氈帽差一一點給風吹　腦袋後去。　　他的心眼裏又納悶着了，望着坐在前一輪黃包車上外甥派來接他的傭人阿二，禁不住又發問：「阿二……阿二哥，那麽高的屋子怎的不會給風吹倒啊」？　　阿二回過頭來朝着他笑子一笑，並沒有告訴他爲什麼高屋子不被風吹倒的原因。看到這一笑，佳福舅舅立刻發覺到自己問得太獃子，一定給外甥的傭人聽了看不起。跟着這想念而來的，他却想到了一件很聰明的掩飾自己土老兒的方法，這方法就是儘管瞧到了什麽希奇的，讓它悶在肚了里，不說出口，人家總不會知道吧。　　呆呆地坐在車子上，半嚮，沒說一句話。不知怎麽一來，又想起他的外甥來了。正泰——外甥是有着十來年沒看見了。　　可是他記得很淸楚，他的妹妹養正泰的時候，是那年……是的，那年十月初七，而且而且記得很淸楚，正泰的鼻子下有着一顆很不小的紅痣。　　眞的，眞的，佳福舅舅他說過：「正泰這孩子有狀元相」！到底他看過幾本相書，他沒有看錯，正泰外甥今日里終於做買辦了，買辦同前淸的狀元是差不多的。　　他曾經抱着正泰走到十里外的橫河壩去買香蕉糖給他吃。　　正泰剛會說話時，就常常喊着：「我要舅舅抱，抱到橫河壩，買糖糖吃」。　　有十來年沒見了，正泰外甥不知道長成一個什麽樣見了。不過，鼻子下的一顆紅痣總可以認得出來的。……　　「舅老爺！到了。」　　黃包車往下一沉，佳福舅舅差一點從墊子上一個跟斗栽不來。他慌忙的朝地上一跳，祇向前冲了幾步，就裝做沒事般的立定了。　　阿二給了車錢，佳福舅舅打算把舖蓋和香籃紮上扁担，何二又向他笑笑：「你別辛苦了，叫人給你拿進去吧說着阿二在一所白色圍牆的大門旁的小東西上拍了一下，大門先開了一個洞，一張烏黑的臉張了一下，這才把大門開了。　　佳福舅舅的眼珠停在他的幾件行李上，阿二看着又笑，他叫頭上紮着紅布的，蛋黑黑的人把行李搬進去，一面領着他走進洋房去。　　剛進洋房的門檻，佳福舅舅脚底下便像踏到香蕉皮般一溜，差一點跌下來。朝地上望一眼，地板紅得發光。　　「格！格！格！」有着三個年靑的女人朝着　笑，他臉皮上立刻發熱啦。阿二却對那些女人使了一個眼色，說：還不快點報告少爺，舅老爺來了。」那些女人便像妖精似的跟進去了。　　佳福舅舅在太師椅上坐下來，當時有人端出茶來，他拿起來呷了一口，怎麽有點苦味，吐出來怕給人笑，祇得縐着眉嚥到肚里。　　好一回，阿二領他到一間很精緻的房裏去，他打算親熱地喊上一句：「正泰」！可是當他看見一個長得白白胖胖的，凸着肚子，穿着外國衣服的小夥子時，他祇不自然的笑了一下。　　是很洪亮的聲音：「你來了嗎？媽到王公館去了。坐坐！」　　佳福舅舅偷眼望了一下正泰，鼻子下的紅痣已給一條小鬍子遮了。一邊靜靜地坐下。　　正泰的聲音突然放低了：「生意我已給，找到了。可是你得留心，別到處的對人說你是我的舅舅！」　　佳福舅舅呆住了。……狀元相……他想着。播音歌曲介紹　　最後五分鐘　　好男兒，意志濃，努力向前攻，不要怕，自己窮，祇要肯用功，經騐足，思想豐，爲國作良楝，本領强，犧牲重，方得逞英雄。一分鐘，二分鐘，三分鐘，怱忽四分鐘，不怕死，向前衝，努力吧，最後五分鐘。　　好男兒，醒悟吧，別在深夢中，國將亡，家將破，莫做糊塗蟲，電影院，戲塲中，，金錢糜費重，靑春去，不返重，轉眼變老翁。一分鐘，二分鐘，三分鐘，怱怱四分鐘，不怕死，向前衝，努力吧，最後五分鐘。　　好男兒，膽量大，體魄健又勇，爲國家，舉槍桿，風盡强暴凶，新生活，時學從，條條關國，要努力？要自重，且勿胡亂　。一分鐘，二分鐘三分鐘，怱忽四分鐘，不怕死，向前衝，努力吧，最後五分鐘。歌唱　　明梅團　　華（一〇六〇）下午三時三刻至四時半　　體育皇后（純美）市上山歌（桃桃）醉臥沙場（張素貞）銀漢雙星（純美）夢中遠別（桃桃）一封快信（張素貞）　　時代歌劇播音社　　佛音（九八〇）下午五時至五時三刻　　愛的花（王琪）賣花詞（林驚）小　哥（芳蘭）（林鶯）大路（劍魂）賣夜來香（芳蘭）我當初認識你（王琪）太平花（林鶯）田家樂（叔牙）春潮回來吧（芳蘭）（叔牙）畢業歌（全體）話劇　　下午六時半至七時一刻　　林秀雲，又是一位環境的被迫，舊式婚姻的犧牲者，她怎樣去抵抗這萬惡的……　　美玲團　　富星（九二〇）下午五時一刻至六時　　小姐我要你的一切（英英）塞外村女（佩佩）長記得（綠茵）（自由神）搖籃歌（靜美）春又來（程瑩）警變（佩佩）蛾眉月（綠茵）這回事情太稀奇（賴玲）　　丁香社　　利利（一二四〇）下午七時一刻至八時　　塞外村女（鄭霞）愛的花（麗亞）愛之炸裂（綠茵）夜花園內（姚莉）夜月之歌（鄭霞）夜深深（麗亞）長記得（綠茵）牧美女（姚莉）　　東陸（六四〇）下午八時至八時一刻　　空中音樂（俞月明）夜月之歌（姚英）夜來香（綠茵）花花世界（姚莉）拒絕（俞月明）放在心頭（姚英和平歌（綠茵）珍珠米（姚莉）　　星光社　　華光（一四八〇）下午七時三刻至八時半　　蝴蝶姑娘（周璐）花生米魏莉）路柳牆花（黃喋）小東西（亭亭）太平花（周璐）從軍別愛（魏莉）恭賀新禧（黃喋）教我如何不想他（亭亭）　　大上海社　　華美（一〇六〇）下午九時至十時　　INeverhadAChange（前奏曲）乳娘曲（王琪）睡的贊美（飛虹）粉紅的夢（飛亞）銀漢　學（莫賓）（王琪）努力（飛　）鴛鴦怨（飛亞）彈詞　　夏荷生三笑　　敦本（八〇〇）下午七時至八時　　開篇「怡紅公子」　　一枝頑石已通靈。不覺紅樓入夢魂。富貴人家倜儻子。依依兒女種情根。大觀園　怡紅院。彼此嫌疑不避人。侍女無一不輕盈。朝夕不離諸姊妹。憐香惜玉暗消魂。有時節猜詩謎。有時節理瑤琴。有時節。海棠花下共論文。枕霞舊友新題號。公子怡紅別有春。蕉下客。檻外人。潇湘子。蘅蕪君。都是那嬝嬝婷婷的姊妹們。桃花面對梨花貌。藕絲杉映柳絲裙。秦世阿房道何足。魏朝銅雀不須云。自從倩女離塵後。似醉如痴悟道形。病雖是病原非病。情到無情倍有情。痴情公子逃禪去。隨了那。渺渺茫茫兩道人。頓將慧劍斬紅塵。紅樓有境無非夢。一枕榮華二十春。痴男痴女最有情。　　邢瑞亭釵頭鳳　　惠靈（一三八〇）下午九時至十時　　開篇「惠山風景綫」　　春來萬紫與千紅。最愛梁溪三月中。小金山。四面淸波浪。水中軒。相對玉皇宮。五里街上多淸雅。一枝楊柳隔桃紅。泉勝舞出龍頭口。泥人造得眞玲瓏。不二法門多是燒香客。誦粉樓上坐美姣容。昭忠祠內留古蹟。香花橋上客相逢。竹爐山房在二泉側。印心石坐對仙洞。壁上吟書古人作。點易台前邵莊公。你看泉。我看松。有人盡上九龍峯。頭茅峯。二茅峯。三茅峯下白雲洞。張仙殿。紫薇宮。諭塋造在正山峯。沿山多是墳墓地。保墓局內不容情。人傑地靈在河塘上。忠節坊造密重重。寶善橋多少風流女。溪山第一曲攔紅。秦園相對錫山塔。映山庵尼姑小春風。各姓祠堂留蹤跡。春秋二祭拜祖宗。千載流傳佳話中。美術　　毛執中美術議習座　　航業（一一八〇）下午五時半至六時一刻　　書畫辭要淺絳」，輕施赭「描法」一，鐵綫描，行雲流水描，三，橄欖描，四，棗核描，五，戰筆水絞描，六，减筆描，七，柳葉描，八，竹葉描，九，混描，十，撅頭釘描，十一，枯筆描，十二，蚯蚓描，十三，高古游絲描，十四，琴弦描，十五，馬蝗描，十六，釘頭鼠尾描，十七，曹衣描，十八，圻蘆描。（二）敎授「無綫電敎中西畫講義」餘音　　時代歌劇社由金兮先生改編之桃花扇，十一月一日由電機上播出。又時代社備有話劇組照片一束，聽衆能解答某問題無誤者，贈送一張。（時代）　　「老闆娘」前日為了廣告費問題，致與捧她場面的××無綫電研究社老閭發生口角。　　時常在無綫電中聽到有「洋瓶先生」，其實是新牌燕燕社的提琴師楊萍，據說他也很喜歡唱。　　純美已嫁給明梅團了，從此不做野雞歌星。　　歌星安娜是個忙人，她每天上午在學校讀害，下午到ＳＴＣ去辦事，晚上又到電臺裏去播音，很遲回家。（以上蕭斯）　　由紅光藝友社改名紅光社社長吳君展達會向紀者云，十月十日起開始播長節目　　前維也納歌詠社社長張乙　君，（該社今已解散）常至大世界內飛燕舞廳狂舞　　小歌星許玲玲辭去商學社之長期節目　　銀雨和銅雷，名雖二個，乃一人也。據探聽原來是張××先生，不知對否？（先生善於打「問路石」，甚爲得體。編者）　　上海老西門外唐家灣厚德里口歌星晝報社出版之「歌星畫報」。第四期原定十一月一日準時問世。現悉該社爲求內容增厚。成爲全國歌詠界之極完美的定期刊物起見，故本期封面改用四色版精印。係海上著名紅歌星黎明健小姐。內容歌星圖照，由該社虞嘉麟君特攝，總計有各歌星最新姿態之傑作八十餘幀，文字方面篇幅亦校前增加。因此編排費時，不得巳將展期至十一月下旬出版，全書約五十餘頁，裝訂一大厚冊，售價照舊每册仍售大洋二角，定閱全年十二册大洋二元四角，加贈歌星原底照相四大幀。倘試閱前出三期，附洋四角即奉，又訊該社所贈定戶歌星照相，完全由滬江照相館特攝，並由各大歌星親　簽名，故名貴非常。

明梅團主任張索貞小姐，前曾因某種關係而為上海世界雲霞歌舞團服務數天，外界不明，成攻擊謂其出賣大腿肉感等，現張索貞小姐為闢謠起見，已有本月廿日停演矣。　　商學社基本社員金儀小姐：（以下刪除。編者）　　陳文元君，現因在某種特殊情形之下，將退出淸萍社。　　百樂門社長儷影小姐，某日偕某君共赴　東飯店五樓大光明照相館取照　　上海歌劇社社員周潔小姐，在播音室裏，喜歡在人家歌唱時，合着拍子跳舞，因為她實在是個能歌遜舞的姑娘啊。（以上夢影）電影「凱歌」中的一段鬬爭史  白木　　龍王行宮，香火鼎盛，人聲沸騰，爆竹聲，鑼鼓聲，踏高蹺，絲竹班，熱鬧之狀，得未曾有。這天是龍王爺要出會，因為數月以來天未曾下過一點雨，禾枯水渴，秋收已成絕望。此時鄉紳李君磐及廟祝梁篤生便大肆活動，居然煽動得一般智識淺薄的愚農鄉婦，咸都埋怨起那敎洋書的鄉村中唯一小學敎員魏鶴齡的欺神滅像，而認為天不下雨，是因他敎了他們子弟不相信龍王爺，所以龍王爺才不肯下雨。　　這一天，卽是彼等對龍王爺表示再度的忠誠，同時更口口聲聲喊着要替龍王爺報仇，在出會的中途去打毁那個學校。　　然而，結果是怎樣呢？這富于緊張而又極盡變幻莫測的局面，藝華公司有聲鉅片，下萬蒼導演的「凱歌」將會給你一個非常沉痛的刺激。銀色雜筆  之爾　　「風雲兒女」許幸之，自從與『肉感鏡頸」陸霞明同居之後，我們除了知道他在着手第二部「牧歌」的工作之外，其他方商關於此公久久毫無消息。最近，因為「牧歌」還非緊張時期，據說許辛之抽暇到揚州故鄉去了。　　到揚州去幹什麼呢？一則，望望高堂老母，二則，向家庭說明終身大事去。　　等許辛之回來，許陸的公開喜酒，大概是逃不掉了。　　「復活」劇本，已山唐納根據原作改編完竣，一待「巡按」出巡之後，電通方面即將積極排練云。　　有人說：「海葬」如果不是天一出品而是別家公司的出品的話，賣座一定比現在好多，此無他，天一公司的牌于在觀衆間已「做煞」了也。　　在沒落中的中國影業，這一點我們應該非常注意的。　　「影評人」和「生意眼」，這二個名詞現在都「罪孽深重」得很，其實我們要不是帶有色眼鏡出看，這二個名詞都並非「大惡不赦」的。

申報建築周刊我國古代建築略說（下）  史東　　次就我國建築物之種類而言，亦甚豐富而複雜。在世界上文化較早的各國，大都是宗敎建築先發達，然而我國則宮廷建築之發達先於宗敎建築以前。並且在昔時，我國的宗敎建築與宮廷建築以及普通住宅之建築，於形式上均無甚差異，亦是我國古代建築之一大特點。換言之，在我國是先有宮廷建築之發達，然後始有宗敎建築，嗣後兩者又並行逐漸發達。我國古代建築物之種類，大別如下：　　（甲）宗敎的建築　　一，廟壇　　二，佛敎建築（如佛寺廟塔之類）　　三，道敎建築（如道觀，風水塔之類）　　四，儒敎建築（如文廟，書院之類）　　五，廟祠　　六，回敎建築（如淸奠寺之類）　　七，陵墓　　（乙）非宗敎的建築　　一，城堡　　二，宮殿，樓閣　　三，住宅，商店　　四，公共建築物（劇塲，會館，衙門之類）　　五，牌樓，門，關之類　　六，石碑　　七，橋　　又如果依我國建築之史的發展，加以時代的區劃，亦可效法諸藝術史，而分爲八個時代。卽；　　一，石器時代……至夏之中期止（西歷紀元前二〇〇〇年以前）　　二，銅器時代……至周之初期止（西歷紀元前一〇〇〇年以前）　　三，銅鐵時代……至漢之初期止（西歷紀元前二〇〇年以前）　　四，漢藝術發達時代……秦漢時代（紀元前二五五—後二二一）　　五，西域藝術攝取時代…朝時代（紀元二二一年—六一八年）　　六，極盛時……唐代（紀元六一八—九六〇年）　　七，寰頹時……宋代（紀元九六〇—一二八〇年）元代（紀元一二八〇—一三六三年）　　八，復興時代……明代（一三六三—一六四四年）　　淸代（一六四四—一九一一年）　　關於年代的分法，常因各家意見之不同而略有差異，所以上表祇可以說是示出時代內容與年代而已。此外，我國建築史雙可分為前後二期，以漢以前為前期，六朝以後為後期。前其為漢族特有的藝術發達時代，後期則為佛教傳入我國以後，我國建築術，受諸外國之影響後的時代。建築行話（二十）  梅震寰　　—關於築塲裏用—　　拌板！遇到倣水門汀工程，除了用車拌（就是滾筒裏拌，詳前）之外，就是手拌，（詳前）手拌難免拌板，所以拌板的解說，就是拌水門汀的一塊板。　　淘灰沙！對於灰沙的意思，先前已經講過，如今單說淘灰沙，淘灰沙在築塲裏並不是指的一伴物事，而指的一個人，因爲築塲裏是非常擾雜的，一帮一帮的做手，誰都叫不出誰的名字，於是就用了他的本身所司的職務而推定之，淘灰沙三字就是指的是一個人，他如看工先生。小先生（崇明地方的工匠稱築塲裏的練習生叫小先生。）翻樣司務，關切司務，小工頭，長工，銅匠司務，開車司務（就是開滾水門汀滾筒使之旋轉的馬達機關者。）等等。都有不名而以職務上的稱呼而稱呼的。　　量方！什麽叫做量方，大凡築塲裏可以以量算的方法决定其數之多寡的，皆得量其方，量方就是量出方數來。方數是、一百方尺變成的，高和闊的相乘數是平方，如一百方尺卽一平方。高和闊相乘再乘長就是立方，如一百方尺卽一立方。平方是算面積，立方是算體積。築塲裏如地板，屋面，墻，皆以平方計算。水門汀大料，柱子，樓板等皆以立方計算。所以初學營造的人，第一對於量方也應該弄淸楚些。　　交邊！在分隔墻的出屋頂的尺把高的牆頂，就叫做交邊。沿詹口那邊的就是產牌。（詳前）對於有交邊的那堍墻也叫作風火牆。（待續）磚拱之研究  穉雲　　在沒有寫正文之前，先來說一說磚拱的定義，用磚來砌成的各種弧形，謂之磚拱，建築在二端磚柱之間，由二端磚柱支持之磚拱須能支持其上面全部磚工的建築重量，須注意下列三點：　　（一）支持的磚柱，須能安全承受並抵抗磚拱傾倒之力。　　（二）必須相當的深度，以抵制上部的壓力不致損壞。　　（三）必須有相當的面積，以防止其壓倒。　　知道了上面的幾點，我們再來談磚拱的種類。　　磚拱可分爲兩種，卽粗造粗磚拱和平整磚拱，後者又可分爲斧製和磨光磚拱二種。　　（一）粗製磚拱——粗製拱磚以普通磚塊所砌，因磚塊之斷面爲長方形，所以嵌塡的灰漿成契狀，因欲避免磚塊之後端相距過大，决無露側而砌，維橫砌成半塊磚原之圈狀弧而已。組糙磚拱專供砌於平整磚拱之後部，或木楣之上，以防止木遭火災燒毀，可用以支持上部之磚工，爲其主要功用。　　（二）反向磚拱——也爲一種粗糙磚拱，伸展於兩中間支柱之間，以承受磚拱所受上部建築之壓力，但此可以發生不平均之抵抗，由於泥土之性質不同或各牆之重量不同而致，其優點之分佈壓力於磚拱全部，而後傳之於泥土。　　（三）平整磚拱—用於窗戶及門檻之上部，常用整磚砌成，其底邊雖平，但偶門過闊時，必須有相當之拱度，以防止砌築時陷落之虞，普通爲每闊一英尺，升高八分之一英寸，此磚拱爲三層至四層磚拱，用特製磚砌成，如用普通磚砌時，也須修琢成適當的形狀，方可使用。拱頂磚必須位於中央，平分磚拱爲相等之二部分，所以普通傳拱所用的磚數，常爲單數。平整磚拱用整塊磚砌者，僅用於門廊之外部，其內部上方之牆，則由粗糙磚拱或樑承受之，其原度和門廊闊度以闊一英尺，其厚定爲一英寸之比例增加；木楣之上，常磚有預防碍拱，以備木楣爲火燒毀時，支持其上部之磚工。　　（四）部分圓磚拱——决定此磚拱外表之方法，爲簡單幾何學原理之應用，卽爲已知之點，而求經過些三點之弧綫，如設拱廊之闊度爲三英尺，升高爲八英寸，Ａ，Ｂ，Ｃ爲欲求弧綫上之點，Ｃ點　升高之頂點，連結ＡＣ及ＢＣ，而後於其上各作一垂直平分綫ＤＯＥＯ則其交點。卽爲所須求之圓心，而ＡＣＢ卽爲所需求之弧綫，其表面上厚度爲九英寸，十四英寸或任何半塊之倍度，或和牆壁同厚。　　（五）法國式磚拱——此傳拱僅可用於門廊寬度不大之處，但此磚拱爲不堅固之建築，僅以其較爲經濟爲可取之點。　　（六）爐側磚拱——此拱砌於棲板近火爐之側，以防止傳熱，並支承　部之重量。　　上述不過是磚工之大要，同時也應於實　施工的時候，切實注意，冀與學理相符，而求得更良好之效果。

1935.10.29

Fragrant River Incident: Resolution Method Agreed Upon, Shang Zhen's Frequent Consultations Yield Results, Japanese Side Promises to Curb Ronin Activity, Security Forces Enter Xianghe County Seat, Rioters Make Three Demands

(Tianjin) The Second Company of Zhang Qingyu's troops, First Brigade of the War Zone Security Forces, re-entered Xianghe County seat on the 28th morning and peacefully negotiated with riot leader Wu Zhenyi, etc., taking over the county seat. The rioters, influenced by certain parties and due to the limited response from other counties, softened their stance, expressing only three demands: 1. The county government must accept the demand for tax reduction for the populace. 2. Those responsible for this incident must not be held accountable. 3. Adequate compensation must be given to the dead and wounded farmers. If the provincial authorities promise this, they can accept it and release Liu Yaodong, recognizing him as the legitimate county magistrate. The provincial authorities, due to diplomatic relations, are eager to resolve the issue quickly and have accepted the terms. Shang Zhen went to Ping on the night of the 28th to personally oversee the handling of the matter. It is rumored that Xianghe riot leader Wu Zhenyi secretly left the area on the night of the 27th, but his son Zhenhua remains in Xianghe, engaging in clandestine activities. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

(Beiping) Regarding the Xianghe riot, Shang Zhen went to Tianjin and held several discussions with Japanese Army Commander Tada and Chief of Staff Takeshita. As a result, the Japanese ronin among the rioters will be ordered by the Japanese side to withdraw. If the rioters submit, the authorities can offer them a path to rehabilitation without further investigation. To maintain local security, a portion of the security forces is preparing to move in. The central government has been sending telegrams to Shang Zhen for days regarding the Xianghe incident, ordering him to quickly resolve it on the spot and prevent it from spreading. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

(Beiping) The Xianghe incident is about to be resolved. A small detachment of Zhang Qingyu's First Brigade of the Security Forces has been dispatched from Erhe and will soon arrive in Xianghe to maintain order. The former county magistrate, Zhao Zhongpu, abandoned the city and fled and will be investigated. Liu Yaodong is temporarily acting as county magistrate. Xianghe rebel leader Wu Yiting extorted tens of thousands of yuan from merchants, falsely claiming it was for the security forces' expenses, but was actually pocketing the money to prepare for an escape if necessary. The pseudo-Director of Public Security, Gao Suoshan, and Wu Yiting have been secretly meeting in the Xianghe County government for days and are now in a difficult situation. The rebels attempted to unite with other counties to launch a simultaneous uprising, but this failed because the authorities were prepared. It is rumored that the rebels recently attempted to convene a meeting of the leaders of the people's militia from various districts under Xianghe County to announce their governing program, with militia leader Jiang Enliang responsible for convening the meeting. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

(Tianjin) Shang Zhen returned to Ping at 8 p.m. on the 28th. According to him, the Xianghe incident has been resolved diplomatically. Security forces have entered the city to maintain order, and everything is returning to normal. The selection of a county magistrate will be decided after arriving in Ping. Wu Zhenyi has left Xianghe and his whereabouts are unknown. It is said that order has been restored in Xianghe County. It has not yet been confirmed whether Liu Yaodong is in Xianghe city. There is no need for my troops to move in. After staying in Ping for two or three days, I plan to return to Baoding. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

(Beiping) According to reports from Xianghe, Liu Yaodong, the newly appointed county magistrate by the Hebei Provincial Government, is still being monitored by the pseudo-Director Gao in the Public Security Bureau of the City God Temple. Liu suffered minor injuries and is confined to a room with his follower Yang. They are provided with food daily. Liu's follower, Bao, was brutally beaten to death by Wu Yiting and others at Jixianlou, and his body is still abandoned in Tiande Store, with no one to bury it. The situation is extremely dire. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

(Beiping) After the Xianghe civil unrest occurred, the Hebei Provincial Government and the Ji-Mi District Office feared that similar incidents would occur in other counties and issued orders to all county governments and security forces to strengthen their defenses. Although there were occasional attempts by conspirators to incite trouble in various counties, they were unsuccessful due to the authorities' strict precautions. The local areas of Sanhe and Changping are very peaceful. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

(Beiping) Zhang from the Provincial Government, accompanied by two Japanese, arrived in Xianghe this afternoon, entering the city through the east gate. They met with Wu Yiting and An Houqi, ordering them to immediately release Liu Yaodong. Further inquiries are being made. Wu is organizing a security force in Xianghe, and bandits with weapons are joining. Foreign reporters went to Sanhe this morning to inspect. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

(Beiping) The south gate of Xianghe is still closed this morning. People are very frightened. A Japanese plane flew over the county city at 9 a.m. this morning, scouting for a full twenty minutes before flying away. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

(Nanjing) The Xianghe incident has not yet been resolved. Shang Zhen sent another long telegram to the Executive Yuan and the Military Affairs Commission on the evening of the 27th, reporting on the handling methods and the discussions with Tada, the commander of the Japanese garrison in Tianjin. He also stated that no other disturbances had occurred in other counties. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

(Beiping) Hebei Chairman Shang Zhen told people on his way from Tianjin to Ping tonight that the Xianghe rebellion had subsided, the security forces had entered the city today, the rebel leaders had fled, and everything in Xianghe was peaceful. (Reuter's Telegram, 28th)

(Beiping) It was learned today from reliable sources that Hebei Provincial Chairman Shang Zhen has agreed with Tada on a solution to the Xianghe incident. It is said that Tada has promised to use his influence to withdraw the Japanese ronin who are still active in Xianghe. Shang Zhen has agreed to allow the rioters to rehabilitate themselves and will station some of the security forces in the demilitarized zone in Xianghe. Postal workers were refused entry to the city by the rebels today. A few days ago, there were concerns that the Xianghe disturbances would spread to other places, but now it is known that all the rumors are inaccurate. According to reliable Chinese and foreign sources, the plot of the mastermind behind the scenes has failed, like the unsuccessful attempt to seize Beiping in June of this year. It is said that their original plan was to launch simultaneous uprisings in the demilitarized zones on October 20 or between the 22nd and 24th. There were actions in Changping, Wuding, and Sanhe, but they all failed because the county magistrates responded appropriately. When the farmers occupied Xianghe, they distributed some Chinese leaflets, which were printed. Since there is no printing office in Xianghe, their origin is obvious. The leaflets bore the printing date of October 10 and the publication date of October 22, but the "23rd" on the date was changed to "20th" with a pencil. (Reuter's Telegram, 28th)

Chairman Chiang Flies to the Capital, Wu Zhihui and Others Welcome Him at the Airport, Chiang and Yan Xishan Confer at Length

(Nanjing) Chairman Chiang, accompanied by Soong Mei-ling, returned to the capital from Feng in a Junkers aircraft at Shen time on the 28th. Those who welcomed him at the station included Wu Zhihui, Chu Minyi representing President Wang, Li Hongwen representing Yan Xishan, as well as Yang Jie, Xiong Bin, Yao Zong, Zeng Baoqing, etc. The Junkers aircraft landed at the Ming Palace airport at 4:20 p.m., circling the field once before landing. Chairman Chiang and his wife disembarked together, nodding to the welcomers as a greeting, and exchanged brief pleasantries with Wu Zhihui and Li Hongwen before returning to the official residence to rest. Those returning to the capital on the same plane included adjutant Chiang Hsiao-hsien and two others. Other followers arrived in the capital earlier at about 2 p.m. on a Ford aircraft. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

(Nanjing) Yan Xishan rested at his headquarters on the morning of the 28th. Those who visited him in the afternoon included Central Committee member Li Liejun, Zhang Zhiben, and Yan's former subordinates in Beijing. In the afternoon, at 5 p.m., he visited various Central Committee members in the capital with Zhao Pilian and others. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

(Nanjing) Chiang visited Yan Xishan at Kong's residence in the Lingyuan New Village at 5:30 p.m., talking for an hour. He hosted a welcome dinner for Yan that evening, with President Wang, Ye Chucang, and He Yingqin as his guests. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

(Nanjing) With the Sixth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee about to open, Chairman Chiang, along with his wife and entourage, returned to the capital from Fenghua on the 28th morning at about 9 a.m., traveling in two aircraft, a Ford and a Junkers. The entourage took the Ford plane first. Chiang and his wife, along with adjutant Chiang Hsiao-hsien and advisor Stinnes, followed in the Junkers aircraft. The Ford aircraft arrived first at 2:20 p.m., and the Junkers aircraft also landed safely at the airport at 4:20 p.m. Those who went to the airport to welcome him included Wu Zhihui, Chu Minyi, Yang Jie, and Li Hongwen representing Yan Xishan. After Chiang disembarked, he nodded to the welcoming personnel as a greeting and spoke briefly with Wu. Li also reported to Chiang that Yan was going to the military academy to pay his respects. Chiang immediately told him that he would rest at the military academy and visit the mausoleum after half an hour. Chiang and his wife then returned to the official residence of the military academy by car. At 5 p.m., he went to Kong's residence to meet with Yan. Coincidentally, Yan also went to the military academy. After Chiang returned to the military academy, Yan hurried over to meet him, and they had a long and cheerful conversation. (Central News Agency Telegram, 28th)

(Ningbo) Chairman Chiang, accompanied by Madam Soong Mei-ling, took a car from Xikou to the Zhenhai Nanhong Airport at 8:45 a.m. on the 28th, taking a Ford aircraft to fly to the capital. Navy Minister Chen Shaokuan accompanied him. Also, President of the Judicial Yuan, Ju Zheng, left Ningbo for Shanghai on the Ningxing steamer at 4 p.m. on the 28th. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

Li Liejun Discusses Southwest Issues: Reaching a Harmonious State

(Nanjing) Li Liejun said, regarding the southwest issue, I have learned from the central government that it has reached a harmonious state. The central government has agreed to consider and adopt several points that the southwest authorities hope for. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

(Nanjing) Li Liejun arrived in the capital with his secretary, Zhang Migong, to attend the Sixth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee. He first visited various Central Committee members at the Central Party Headquarters to confer. Li told visitors that he had come to the capital despite his illness to participate in the Sixth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee, hoping to contribute his personal views to the party and the nation. He had discussed the proposals for the conference with various committee members in Shanghai and waited to solicit the signatures of various committee members in the capital before sending them to the secretariat. Mr. Feng Huanzhang's proposal was previously entrusted to me to bring to Shanghai, but now Feng himself intends to revise it and has already returned it. As for whether Feng will come to the capital to attend, he had previously indicated that he planned to come to the capital, but there has been no news recently. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

Half of the Fifth National Congress Overseas Representatives Arrive in the Capital

(Nanjing) According to political circles, half of the representatives from various overseas ports attending the congress have arrived in the capital. Travel expenses are allocated by the central government, with the amount determined by the distance of the journey. The furthest are about 2,000 yuan per person, and the total travel expenses are about 100,000 yuan. In addition, meal expenses during the conference will also be fully supplied by the central government. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

(Hong Kong) The Executive Department held a meeting on the morning of the 28th. Xiao Focheng was absent due to illness. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

(Beiping) A spokesperson for the Mongolian Political Council's office in Beiping stated that Wu He, Le Tao, Ni Guanzhou, Yideqin, and Bao Yueqing, the director of this office, will come to Ping this week. In response to a central government telegram, they will rush to Nanjing before next month. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

Our Formal Response to the League of Nations Regarding Sanctions

(Nanjing) After being notified by the League of Nations regarding the proposed sanctions against Italy, our country has carefully studied and considered the matter and has formally responded to the League of Nations. However, the content must wait for the League of Nations to publish it. (Central News Agency Telegram, 28th)

(Nanjing) It is confirmed by diplomatic circles that after the League of Nations resolution to notify member states of sanctions against Italy, our government has carefully considered this and, as of yesterday, has formally replied to the League of Nations. The content and wording of this notice must be released by the League of Nations Secretariat after it is received. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

Central Government and National Government Jointly Commemorate This Week

(Nanjing) The central government and national government jointly held a memorial week at 9 a.m. on the 28th. Those who attended included Central Committee members Yu Youren, Chen Guofu, Ye Chucang, Li Liejun, Bai Wenwei, Wang Bailing, Miao Peicheng, Li Zonghuang, Deng Jiayan, Zhang Ji, Wang Qi, Ma Chaojun, Hong Ludong, Shi Ying, Li Fulin, Zeng Kuoqing, and heads of various departments and bureaus of the national government Wei Huai, Lü Chao, Chen Qicai, Yang Rumei, Wen Yiyou, Zhu Wenzhong, Xiao Qin, Fu Xuanqing, and about 600 staff members from the Yuan and ministries. Chen Guofu presided over the meeting. Zhang Zhiben reported on the true meaning of unity, stating that it should be based on mutual understanding and trust. Those who can understand each other must be strict with themselves and lenient with others. Those who can trust each other must first have a shared faith. Only in this way can we achieve sincere unity and jointly shoulder the important task of saving the country. The meeting adjourned at 9:20 a.m. (Central News Agency Telegram, 28th)

Constitutional Draft Amendment: Yellow Book Submitted to Plenary Session, to Be Promulgated and Implemented After Approval by the National Assembly

(Nanjing) The constitutional draft amendment passed by the Legislative Yuan this time has been printed into a yellow book. On the 28th, a letter was sent to the Central Secretariat, which will then forward it to the Standing Committee for submission to the Sixth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee for discussion. After being approved by the Sixth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee, it must also be submitted to the Fifth Plenary Session of the National Congress and the National Assembly for discussion. Finally, it will be promulgated and implemented after being approved by the National Assembly. (Central News Agency Telegram, 28th)

Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Committee Passes Electrical Loan

(Nanjing) The Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Board of Directors held its 34th meeting on the 28th, with Zhu Jiahua and others attending. Resolutions: (1) The Ministry of Industry's Wenxi Paper Mill loan case will be further discussed next time. (2) The Capital Power Plant and Electrical Testing Institute loan case passed. (3) The Preparatory Office of the Central Museum is requested to allocate construction funds; 150,000 yuan of the previous year's subsidy will be allocated first. (4) The allocation of academic disciplines for the fourth round of students studying in the UK at public expense is set at 21 places; detailed measures will be announced after the regulations are formulated. (5) Draft rules for soliciting junior high school history and geography textbooks passed. (Central News Agency Telegram, 28th)

Yin Rugeng Returns to Tianjin from Changchun

(Tianjin) Yin Rugeng returned to Tianjin from Changchun on the morning of the 28th and immediately discussed security issues within the war zone with Takeshita, the head of the Shanhaiguan Special Service Agency. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

Japanese Army to Hold Autumn Military Exercise Near Beiping and Tianjin

(Beiping) The Beiping Municipal Government received a notice today from the Japanese Tianjin Garrison Headquarters, stating that the Japanese army will conduct its routine autumn exercise near Beiping and Tianjin in early November. From the evening of November 4th to 6th, the exercise will take place in the area near Yuan, Tai, Changxindian, Liangxiang, Huangcun, and Wanzhuang, and will camp in Huangcun and Liangxiang. From the morning of the 6th to the 7th, the exercise will take place in the area near Junliangcheng in Tianjin, and will camp in Tianjin. During the exercise, both day and night, artillery and machine guns will be used for blank firing. It is hoped that the general officials and people will be notified so that there will be no misunderstandings at that time and that convenience will be provided. According to the letter, in addition to reporting and informing by telegram, the Municipal Government has also ordered the Public Security Bureau to forward instructions to the district offices to inform nearby residents to be aware of the matter. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

(Tianjin) A platoon of Japanese infantrymen in Tianjin conducted street fighting exercises in Nanshi Rongan Street at 10 a.m. on the 28th, using the gate of the Lu residence across from Ronghou Lane as a fortress. They fired smoke bombs, throwing a total of four, of which three exploded. One did not explode at the time, and three soldiers went to inspect it. Unexpectedly, it exploded suddenly, injuring the heads and faces of the three soldiers. The exercise was stopped immediately and they were carried back to the Haiguang Temple barracks. Over a hundred fully armed Japanese soldiers from the Tianjin garrison paraded on Dongmalu and Hebei Avenue from Haiguang Temple at 10 a.m. on the 28th, returning to the barracks at noon. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

Shima and Nishida Fly to Chahar and Suiyuan for Inspection

Total Central Government Tax Revenue

(Nanjing) According to the Tax Department of the Ministry of Finance, the index of central government tax revenues is as follows: Customs duties are budgeted at over 350 million yuan for the 24th year, salt tax is over 180 million yuan, and consolidated tax is over 110 million yuan. These three major taxes total about 650 million yuan. The remaining taxes are less than 10 million yuan. The total central government tax revenue is less than 700 million yuan. On the expenditure side, military expenses account for the largest share, at over 300 million yuan, followed by debt service, accounting for 38%. The remainder is used for party fees, political expenses, and education and cultural construction. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

Changlu Tax Police Bureau Transfers Troops to Suppress Nitrate Miners in Pingxiang

(Tianjin) The nitrate miners in Pingxiang, southern Hebei, incited by Shi You, Yue Guitang, have regrouped several hundred people with complete uniforms and weapons, calling themselves the Regular Army. There are still over a thousand nitrate miners who have agreed that when the tax police come to attack, they will immediately gather to resist, calling themselves the Reserve Army. Zhou, the Chief of the Changlu Tax Police, telegraphed Haizhou, transferring a large detachment of tax police to suppress them. A regiment of Sun Dequan's division stationed in Xingtai began moving towards Pingxiang on the 26th. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

Economic Commission Transfers Funds to Shandong for Dike Construction

(Jinan) Han Fuju returned to Jinan today. The Economic Commission transferred 200,000 yuan for dike construction. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

(Jinan) Zhou Li, the director of the dike construction project, took the dike construction plan to Beijing some days ago and presented it to the Economic Commission in person. He returned to Jinan yesterday. According to him, the Economic Commission expressed considerable agreement with the plan, but in order to save public funds, it plans to prioritize urgent matters and appropriately reduce the river diversion and other post-disaster projects. Zhang Honglie said that all the projects are necessary. If they are reduced again, I cannot be responsible. After the Fifth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee, he plans to go to Beijing to make final consultations with the Economic Commission. Also, the Jiangsu dam enclosure and new dam base project are scheduled to be tendered on the 29th. Li Sheng has completed the five sections of the secret swept dam. The Ge dike in Juye collapsed severely due to the storm the night before. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

Tianjin County to Implement Winter Defense Immediately

(Tianjin) Chen Zhongyue, the magistrate of Tianjin County, said that the area around Haixia and Xianshui is as peaceful as ever. Although there are rumors from the outside, they are not true. Although pseudo-organizations and leaflets provoking neighboring countries and sentiments similar to the Communist Party have been discovered previously, they have not been seen recently due to strict precautions. In order to prevent accidents, Tianjin County plans to implement winter defense immediately. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

Steep Drop in Water Level in the Central Canal, Two Boat Capsizings Resulting in Multiple Drownings

(Qingjiangpu) According to the Huaiyin District Office and the Flood Control Office, the water level in the Central Canal has dropped sharply by three feet since Frost's Descent (October 23rd). Also, a boat of Jiang Wu was overturned by wind and waves while passing through the Yangzhuang Shuangjin Sluice, drowning 17 passengers on board. A ferry at Zhangdian in the lower reaches of the Salt River also killed more than 20 people. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

(Xuzhou) According to reports from Suqian, after the Dongshui Dam in the Central Canal was dismantled and released, the water level in Luoma Lake dropped. According to the latest situation, it is hoped that wheat can be planted in the dried lakebed. Haishu has also telegraphed for days to report that the water is stable. However, due to the tidal ebb and flow, the levee is still under construction. The Donghai County Government has sent craftsmen into the mountains to cut down 20,000 pine piles for flood prevention. Bandit ships are rampant in the Guanshu area, with multiple incidents of robbing taking place on the water every day. The District Office has strictly ordered suppression. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

Water Level Drops in Guanyun

(Xuzhou) The county seat of Guanyun is surrounded by floods on three sides, and the earthen base city embankment is gradually being soaked through. The Salt Affairs Inspection Office has obtained approval from the Ministry of Finance to allocate funds to help repair the city wall. Together with the large number of sacks purchased by County Magistrate Xu, they are being piled higher and thicker. At the same time, a portion of the salt flats on the east bank of the Salt River has been flooded. Salt farmers are desperately protecting the salt fields and people's embankments. Fortunately, the water level has dropped in recent days, the dangerous period is about to pass, and people's hearts are slightly at ease. (Central News Agency Telegram, 28th)

Northwest Two Townships of Xunling Placed Under Jurisdiction of Huangmei

(Hankou) After investigation by representatives from the central government and the three provinces on the border of Hubei, Anhui and Jiangxi, an initial decision was made at the Xunling Conference to place the northwest two townships of Xunling under the jurisdiction of Huangmei in Hubei. The provincial government, considering that Huangmei's jurisdiction is extensive after the annexation of the two townships, has decided to add another county in the area below Kongxi and bordering Susong in the county, in order to facilitate governance. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

Huainan Railway to Open Next Month (Nanjing)

The section of the Huainan Railway between Hechao has already been opened last month. The track-laying project from Chaoxian to Yuxi terminus is underway, and the Jiangbian terminal has been completed. It is scheduled to be fully opened next month. (28th Central News Agency dispatch)

Zhejiang Silversmiths Attempt to Ship Silver Ornaments to Shanghai, Customs Refuses to Issue Export Permits (Nanjing)

Silversmiths in Zhejiang Province planned to ship silver ornaments to Shanghai for sale and declared them to Hangzhou Customs. However, the customs believed that silver ornaments should only be sold to the mint and instructed them to contact the Hangzhou Central Branch and refused to issue export permits. (28th Special Dispatch)

Senior Civil Service Examination Committee to Be Sworn in Within Days (Nanjing)

Disallowed to Be Handled by Administrative Offices (Nanjing)

Various chambers of commerce have petitioned the Ministry of Finance, requesting that ordinary violations of the stamp tax law be handled by administrative offices to show consideration. It is now learned that the Ministry of Finance believes that the so-called "ordinary cases" are difficult to define and that the same case should not have two different handling methods. Therefore, the previous request has been rejected. (28th Central News Agency dispatch)

Ministry of Finance Orders Sichuan Province to Change Special Tax on Kerosene to Unified Tax (Nanjing)

Sichuan Province has been levying a special tax on kerosene. The central government instructed that it be changed to a unified tax and that the special tax be discontinued. Recently, the Ministry of Finance received reports from Mobil and Asiatic that the Sichuan Special Tax Bureau has not stopped levying the special tax. The Ministry of Finance has ordered the special envoy stationed in Sichuan to strictly comply with the instructions on the 28th. (28th Special Dispatch)

Zhang Yuanfu Discusses Trade with New Russia (Nanjing)

Xinjiang Representative Zhang Yuanfu stated that the rumors of New Russia taking out a loan in Qincai were slightly inaccurate. Commissioner Gao came to Nanjing and explained that trade with New Russia was previously based on barter. However, in recent years, as Xinjiang's industry has gradually developed, its purchases from Russia have decreased. Russia needs to purchase local goods such as raw leather and fur in Xinjiang and requested advance payment, but this has not been realized. The restoration of the Dihua route by the Eurasia Company previously faced difficulties. Currently, the value of the Ruble fluctuates with the US dollar. Trade between Xinjiang and the Soviet Union is relatively frequent, so the exchange rate is based on the US dollar. The Xin-Sui automobile runs once a month, costing ten yuan each time, with little freight. Governor Sheng Shicai ordered Yu to be stationed in Nanjing, which Yu is still considering. Sheng himself will not come to Nanjing for the time being due to transportation inconvenience. (28th)

Ministry of Transportation to Crack Down on Small Inland Steamers Operating Without Permits (Nanjing)

The Ministry of Transportation has discovered that many small inland steamers are operating without permits. On the 28th, it informed the provincial governments to instruct county governments and maritime police to inspect all small steamers operating on inland rivers for permits. Those operating without permits will be immediately banned and ordered to apply for permits from the Ministry. (28th Special Dispatch)

Various Circles in Beiping Return from Inspection Tour of Japan (Beiping)

The 304th through train from Beiping to Baotou on the Ping Sui Railway, organized by the Beiping Municipal Government for various circles to inspect Japan, derailed yesterday morning between Qinglongqiao and Nankou after departing from Baotou. The axle of the guard car suddenly broke, and the train stopped immediately. The railway bureau, upon hearing the news, immediately sent an engineering train to rush to repair it, which was completed at about 9:00 a.m. Fortunately, there were no casualties. The train arrived in Beiping this afternoon, delayed by four hours. (18th Special Dispatch)

At 7:00 p.m. on the 28th, eighteen people dressed as plainclothes from a certain country, led by a Chinese person, suddenly arrived at the Tianjin News Inspection Office. Unprecedented Great Floods in the United States and Central America, Honduras and Haiti

Tegucigalpa

Refugees who have walked to the capital today bring news of an unprecedented disaster in Honduras. They claim that the rivers have overflowed, flooding the towns of La Ceiba, Choloma, Quimistan, and Progreso. Hundreds of homes are submerged, and people are rushing to safety. The water in Progreso is 59 feet deep. It is believed that many people and animals have drowned, but it will take time to report the number of deaths because transportation is blocked by the wind and floods. (27th Guomin Dian)

Port-au-Prince, Haiti

Floods have occurred in southern Haiti. It is learned that up to two thousand people have died, and thousands of victims are currently homeless. (27th Havas Dian)

Fascist Party Revolution Anniversary, Italy Celebrates National Holiday, Prime Minister Encourages Blackshirt Comrades to Persevere (Rome)

Today is the 13th anniversary of the Fascist Party's March on Rome. The national celebration ceremony was held in gloomy weather and a solemn atmosphere, like a religious ceremony. Prime Minister Mussolini gave a speech in the portico of the Palazzo Venezia at 10:00 a.m., saying, "Today is the beginning of the fourteenth year of the Fascist Party's rule. We should move forward with the same courage." The city was decorated with flags and banners, and all stores were closed for the day to celebrate. In the morning, Fascist Party cadres went to the Verano cemetery to lay flowers in honor of the revolutionary martyrs. Then, they held a Mass at the Foti Church in the Palazzo Braschi, the party headquarters. Nobles and members of the party's Rome section attended. After the ceremony, 300 veteran party members (those who joined the party before the Roman election) and 300 young party members, divided into six teams of 100 each, carried the large flag of the Palazzo Braschi to the Palazzo Venezia. When they reached the front of the palace, they held a flag-raising ceremony. The crowd sang revolutionary songs and asked Prime Minister Mussolini to come and receive their congratulations. The Prime Minister arrived in party military uniform, and the crowd applauded and cheered. The Prime Minister gave a short speech, saying that the country should have an indomitable spirit and be brave. Then, he went from the Palazzo Venezia to the San Paolo district to preside over the inauguration ceremony of the Pyramid Road. In the evening, the large flag of the Palazzo Braschi was returned to the palace by the original team. In addition to Rome, all cities across the country held similar celebrations. (28th Havas Dian)

Hopes for a Resolution of the Italo-Ethiopian Dispute Are Slim, Britain and France Prepare to Vigorously Enforce Sanctions (London)

Hopes for an early successful resolution of the Italo-Ethiopian dispute seem to have been abandoned today. The British and French governments are preparing to vigorously implement the plan of sanctions against Italy at the meeting of the League of Nations Sanctions Committee on Thursday. (28th Guomin Dian)

(Paris)

It is now known that Britain insists that the first step of sanctions against Italy must be fully implemented on November 15. Britain has also notified the French government that it is unwise to delay the implementation of sanctions. Financial and economic experts at the time believe that if sanctions can be rigorously enforced, Italy may begin peace talks before the end of the year. (28th Guomin Dian)

(Geneva)

The League of Nations previously sought the opinion of the United States on sanctions against Italy. The U.S. reply was delivered to the Secretariat of the League of Nations today by the U.S. Envoy to Switzerland, Mr. Wilson. Representatives of the League of Nations today said that the U.S. reply was diplomatically worded, without making direct statements, as expected. However, the French representative here believes that Britain has inevitably suffered a slight blow. (28th Guomin Dian)

Countries Notify League of Nations of Participation in Sanctions Against Italy, India Decides on Methods Similar to Britain (Geneva)

As of now, 35 member states of the League of Nations have notified the League of Nations that they accept the method of prohibiting the shipment of arms to Italy. Sixteen countries have accepted the financial sanctions plan passed by the League of Nations. Seven countries have banned the import of Italian goods. Seven countries have banned the export of certain raw materials to Italy. Four countries have accepted mutual assistance measures. Since the governments of Britain and France replied to the League of Nations yesterday that they are prepared to implement economic sanctions, people in the League of Nations believe that in these few days, most countries will notify their participation in economic sanctions. (28th Havas Dian)

New Delhi

The Indian government today decided to implement financial and economic sanctions against Italy, with methods almost identical to those implemented by Britain. (28th Reuters Dian)

Belgrade

The Yugoslav government today ordered a ban on the shipment of arms and ammunition to Italy. This move is in compliance with the resolution of the League of Nations sanctions. (27th Guomin Dian)

Oslo

The Norwegian government recently notified the League of Nations that it is prepared to ban the import of Italian goods and the export of horses, metals, and other items to Italy. As for the implementation of economic sanctions, although the Norwegian government is willing to implement them according to the date decided by the League of Nations General Assembly Sanctions Committee, influential sources say that due to various practical difficulties, it may be difficult to put them into effect before mid-November. (28th Havas Dian)

Swiss Capital

The Swiss government today resolved to ban the transport of goods to both Italy and Abyssinia and to implement financial sanctions against Italy. Regarding economic sanctions, the government is now banning the transport of major products to Italy. Since Italy cannot sell goods or immediately pay for the goods purchased, other goods transported from Switzerland to Italy will be offset by the same value of goods imported from Italy to Switzerland according to the clearing system. It is heard that the League of Nations will accept Switzerland's compromise method of fulfilling its obligations under the League of Nations Covenant. (28th Reuters Dian)

East African War Imminent, Italian Army Awaits General Attack, North Road Advances 12 Kilometers, Aiming to Take the City of Makale in One Go (Rome)

According to news here today, Italian troops on both the northern and southern routes will launch a major offensive on Monday, and today's advance is just a preliminary action. As the League of Nations meeting on Thursday will begin to implement economic sanctions against Italy, and the U.S. and Italy had completely given up hope of reaching a diplomatic solution, the entire nation is preparing for the day to celebrate the Fascist Party's march on Rome in 1922. (27th Guomin Dian)

(Rome)

According to political figures, the development prospects of the diplomatic situation are not optimistic, so the Italian army will soon take a real offensive on the East African front. Officials are paying close attention to the negotiations being conducted by Britain and France, but they believe that these negotiations have no hope of success, so Italy has not participated. What Italy is most concerned about at the moment is the military development in Abyssinia. It is heard that the troops led by General Biccheri Piroli on the northern route have advanced 12 kilometers. The area in the Feresmai River basin is already under Italian control. It is generally expected that the city of Makale will be taken in a few days. (28th Havas Dian)

Port of Massawa, Italian Eritrea

Before departing for home last night, the Italian Chief of Staff Badoglio and the Colonial Minister Lessona consulted with the High Commissioner of East Africa, General de Bono, on the Italian army's second offensive plan. It is also heard that in order to minimize casualties, the Italian military authorities have decided to postpone the offensive, and the general attack will not begin until a few days later. (27th Havas Dian)

Italian Army Activities on All Fronts in Preparation for a General Attack, Joining Forces to Penetrate Deep into Abyssinia, Aircraft Reconnaissance and Bombing (Abyssinian Capital)

According to a Reuters dispatch from Asmara, the Blackshirt Brigade led by General Diamanti is making various preparations for a general offensive on the left wing of the Italian army, with important actions already taken. Italian soldiers marched ten miles without resistance and have occupied the village of Adimesas. The Italian vanguard is now lining up along the mountain path of Via Inghilterra. Yesterday, Italian aircraft were very active on the entire front line. Aircraft flew out of Quba and bombarded Abyssinian camps around Magolo, halfway to the Abyssinian capital. Aircraft on the right wing were also conducting extensive reconnaissance in the Sasabene area and dropped bombs wherever Abyssinian soldiers were seen gathering. (27th Reuters Dian)

Asmara

The Italian Shirt Army led by General Diamanti and the Ascari native soldiers led by General Biheqi joined forces today, penetrating deep into Abyssinia and advancing towards Makale in a spearhead formation. The two armies departed from Mount Samayat and marched ten miles to the right without encountering resistance from the Abyssinian army. The left wing of the Italian army has now reached a key pass in Abyssinia like an outstretched arm. A major battle is about to occur, and today's actions by the Italian army have shown that the terrain conditions do not pose an obstacle to military vehicles. Although the progress of the Italian army has slowed down recently, it seems to be due to diplomatic relations. (27th Guomin Dian)

Northern Italian Army Frontline

The northern Italian army is now awaiting orders to attack. The recent advance of the Blackshirt Army by ten miles is actually a consolidation of the defense line, not a general offensive. It is now learned that the Italian army's second offensive will take a curved advance, with the left wing occupying Makale. The center is currently the busiest, with the Blackshirt Army and the natives advancing before the road is completed. Road builders, well drillers, and mule drivers are following closely behind, and engineering teams are exploring resources. The Asmara gold mine will soon reopen. (28th Guomin Dian)

Asmara, Italian Eritrea

Tigray Province Frontline

According to a dispatch from this agency's accompanying journalist, Baer, after occupying Adimeffa and advancing along the Feresmai River, it will not be difficult for the Italian army on the northern route to seize the fertile area in the north, which is rich in water resources. According to the recent actions of the Italian army, its purpose is not only to occupy various strategic locations, but also to occupy the affluent area where the former Emperor Menelik of Abyssinia raised military supplies in the 1896 campaign (i.e., the battle in which the Italian army was defeated in the city of Adwa). At present, a division of native soldiers stationed in the city of Antio is rapidly advancing. There is no difficulty in the march, because the road connecting that city from the rear has been mostly completed, and all military food can be sent directly to the forward troops. (28th Havas Dian)

Instigating a Murder Case: Gu Zhuxuan Sentenced to Fifteen Years Imprisonment, with Ten Years Deprivation of Civil Rights. Accusation First, Money Demanded Later.

Former head of the Zhabei Defense Corps, chairman of the Jianghuai Eight Counties Association in Shanghai, owner of the Tianchan Stage, and native of Yancheng, Gu Zhuxuan, also known as Gu Si Laoban, fifty years old this year, was accused by Zhao Guangfu, a native of Yangzhou, who was convicted in the assassination of Tang Jiapeng, the former manager of the Rongji Game Hall in the Great World, of instigating the murder of Tang. According to Zhao, Gu had met with him in Room 208 of the Asia Hotel on Avenue Edward VII and promised a reward of 10,000 yuan upon completion of the task. Furthermore, Zhang Tinggui, aka Xiao Sizi, a native of Funing and an accomplice of Zhao, testified that he witnessed Gu handing over two pistols at the Asia Hotel. The Judicial Police Department reported this to the Second Special Court, which issued an arrest warrant to the Shanghai Municipal Police. On September 10th, at noon, Chinese and Western detectives were dispatched, first registering at the First Special District Court and then reporting to the Central Police Station of the Public Concession to request assistance from detectives. They proceeded to Gu's residence at No. 9, Yonghe Lane, No. 222 North Xizang Road, arrested Gu, and brought him back to the French Concession Police Department before transferring him to the Second Special Court for interrogation and investigation. The Judicial Police Department, in accordance with Article 29 and Article 271 of the Criminal Law, filed a public prosecution against Gu for instigating murder, requesting legal proceedings. Guo Tang Youmei, the younger sister of the victim Tang Jiapeng, also hired a lawyer to represent her in the proceedings, requesting to reserve the right to file a private suit. During the interrogation, Gu Zhuxuan denied instigating murder, claiming that Zhao Guangfu had repeatedly extorted him with letters, and when unsuccessful, made false accusations out of spite. He hired Xue Dubi, Lin Dawen, and Wu Kaisheng as his defense lawyers. On the afternoon of the 12th of this month, Wang Gangxu, the presiding judge of the Criminal Court, deemed the case significant and, for the sake of prudence, specially accompanied by Associate Judges Xiong Huiping and Zhang Chaozuo, and court clerk Zheng Rong, convened a collegial panel with Prosecutor Wang Ren to conduct a joint trial. They ordered the accuser Zhao Guangfu, and witnesses Zhang Tinggui, Xue Zhenyi, Zhang Shuchuan, and Zhu Jincheng, who were already in custody, to appear in court for questioning and cross-examination. After five hours, the court declared the debate closed and scheduled the pronouncement of the verdict for 2:00 PM on the 18th. After the trial, Judge Wang, along with Associate Judges Xiong and Zhang, convened a meeting of all court presidents and judges to deliberate and begin drafting the judgment. However, Gu Zhuxuan submitted several points of rebuttal in a written statement. The presiding judge, in order to thoroughly understand the case, spared no effort to seek details, with the aim of avoiding any injustice. As a result, the originally scheduled pronouncement of the verdict on the 18th was postponed. The court declared the debate reopened and resumed the trial on the afternoon of the 22nd, summoning witnesses Zhao Quansheng, manager of the Jiangnan Hotel, Zhou Shaolian, bookkeeper of the Asia Hotel, and He Shouming, a former prisoner No. 268 recently released from the Second Special Prison, as well as inmates Zhao Guangfu, Zhang Tingzi, and Zhu Jincheng for detailed questioning and cross-examination, and confronting them with Gu. The court declared the debate closed again and scheduled the pronouncement of the verdict for 2:00 PM on the 28th. These details have been reported in previous newspapers. Yesterday marked the date for the pronouncement of the verdict. From 1:00 PM, the court maintained the same strict security as before. The French Concession Police Department also dispatched a reserve team of Chinese police officers to patrol the perimeter and sent Chinese and Western detectives to the court to maintain order inside and outside the courtroom, as before. Gu's family and related friends arrived at the court before 2:00 PM, obtained tickets to observe the proceedings, and waited in the courtroom. The number of people waiting for the verdict still reached over a hundred, and the courtroom was extremely crowded. Those who arrived later had to stand outside the court to await the news. At 2:30 PM, Judge Wang, accompanied by Associate Judges Xiong and Zhang, and Clerk Zheng, ascended the bench in the First Court to pronounce the verdict. Attorneys Fei Xizhen and Yuan Jiahuang represented the Judicial Police Department. French Vice Consul and Legal Advisor to the French Municipal Council, Jiatang (transliteration), Secretary of the Legal Advisory Office, Li Jiaer (transliteration), and Hu Chongguang, a Chinese French secretary, also attended the hearing. The defendant's defense lawyers Xue Lin Wu (Wu replaced by Shi Honglie) also arrived on time to await instructions. The attorney representing the plaintiff, Guo Tang Youmei, was also present to await the verdict. The atmosphere in the courtroom suddenly became quiet and solemn. The court ordered the bailiffs to bring the defendant Gu Zhuxuan to the stand. Gu was dressed in a gray iron-machine-spun camel hair robe, wearing a melon-skin cap and white socks and satin shoes, standing with his head bowed in the defendant's box. He looked more haggard than before. The court briefly inquired about Gu's age, origin, occupation, and address, and then informed him that the court was ready to pronounce the verdict in the case of the Judicial Police Department's prosecution against him for instigating murder. Judge Wang finished speaking, then rose and read the main text of the verdict, stating, "Gu Zhuxuan is sentenced to fifteen years of imprisonment for instigating murder, with ten years of deprivation of civil rights." After reading the verdict, he briefly explained the reasons for the judgment to Gu, saying that the court, after repeated trials, recognized that Zhao Guangfu's accusation preceded his writing letters to you demanding money, while Zhang Tinggui, an accomplice in the case, did not extort you, but his testimony was the same as Zhao's. Therefore, your criminal suspicion is confirmed. You are sentenced to fifteen years of imprisonment and ten years of deprivation of civil rights. If you do not accept the verdict, you may submit a written appeal to the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court within ten days of receiving the verdict." He also informed him that during the appeal period, he would remain in custody. After the announcement, the court adjourned. Gu remained silent with his head bowed, not uttering a word, and was led away by the bailiffs. The spectators exited the courtroom in a hubbub. When Gu's family and friends heard the verdict of imprisonment, they all looked worried, exchanged glances silently, and left the court in disappointment.

Central District Land: Deadline for Construction, Otherwise a 1% Vacancy Fee Will Be Charged.

The municipal government, in order to promote prosperity in the city center, specially promulgated the "Central District Land Regulations," which stipulate that those who acquire land in the central district must begin construction within one year. Otherwise, a vacancy fee of 2% of the land price will be charged monthly. Due to the January 28th Incident, enforcement was temporarily suspended. Last September, the municipal government meeting discussed the issue again and decided to reduce the vacancy fee to 1% due to the economic downturn. The Central District Land Owners Association submitted a request to the municipal government at the end of September this year to extend the construction deadline and waive the vacancy fee. However, this was rejected by the Central District Construction Committee for the seventy-ninth time. This month, they submitted a second request, which was again rejected by the committee at its eightieth meeting the other day, in order to ensure the prosperity of the city center is not affected.

Wise Shaman Overturns Bandit, Leading to Arrest. Is it the Spirit of the Bodhisattva? Zhao Furong's Family Rejoices. The Bandit is Unlucky. Zhou Bingcheng Takes the Opportunity to Make the Arrest.

Zhao Furong, a native of Huzhou, 45 years old, is a shaman (commonly called a "xianren" or immortal). He and his family rent a two-story house at No. 2 Dasheng Lane, No. 54 Taolefeis Road in the French Concession. He lives there alone. Besides the hall on the second floor, which serves as the immortal's hall, where statues of the Thousand-Hand Guanyin, the Child-Giving Guanyin, the City God, and other deities are enshrined. Zhao claims that he can channel the immortal's power to diagnose illnesses. This has led superstitious men and women to flock to him to seek treatment or divine prescriptions from the statues. As a result, Zhao has accumulated tens of thousands of dollars, becoming a wealthy man, which has attracted the attention of bandits. Yesterday morning at 8:30 AM, Zhao finished washing and knelt before the statues to light incense and candles, chanting scriptures and praying piously. Suddenly, a bandit of about thirty years of age, wearing an old military uniform, knocked on Zhao's door. The servant thought that the visitor was there to seek treatment or a divine prescription and opened the door respectfully. The bandit entered the hall and asked if Mr. Zhao was home. Before the servant could answer, the bandit rushed up to the hall on the second floor and saw Zhao kneeling before the altar. Zhao stood up and asked the bandit why he was there. The bandit went to the window, stood facing inward, took out a pistol, and aimed it at Zhao, claiming, "Mr. Zhao, I met you in Shuanglin before. After I was discharged from the army, I asked you for a loan of 500 yuan, or at least 300 yuan," and continued with threats. Zhao replied that he had never met the bandit before and had no money on him. He asked the bandit to follow him to the back to get money. The bandit believed him and followed Zhao out of the room and stood at the top of the stairs. Zhao turned around, pulled the door to the hall on the second floor shut, turned around, saw the bandit standing at the top of the stairs, and realizing that this was a good opportunity, suddenly pushed the bandit unexpectedly. The bandit lost his balance and fell down the stairs. Zhao shouted "robber" loudly. The neighbors in front heard the shout and blew whistles in response. The bandit realized that the opportunity was lost and, without being able to extort anything, picked up the pistol he had brought and fled. Zhao followed in pursuit. The bandit ran east out of the lane and reached the intersection of Lyuban Road, where he was intercepted by police officers and detective Zhou Bingcheng, who seized the pistol he was carrying. They then found two more pistols in the bandit's crotch. The bandit was taken to the Lujiawan Central Police Station for interrogation, and Zhao followed to report the bandit's extortion. When police officers investigated at Zhao's home after the incident, Zhao's family said that they were fortunate to have the blessings of the Buddha and Bodhisattvas. Although the bandit had a pistol, he did not fire it and no money was stolen. They were grateful to the Bodhisattvas for their protection.

Tan Family Father and Son Dispute. The Official Intends to Postpone Adjudication and Mediate.

Tan Jingyu, the owner of Tan Tongxing, a wealthy Cantonese businessman in Shanghai, resides in Anfu Lane, Haskell Road. He is engaged in real estate and other businesses, with assets exceeding ten million. His son, Tan Zhuo, 34 years old, was dissatisfied with certain actions of his father when he was young and intended to take action. His father discovered this, and in anger, declared the disownment of his son in the newspapers and filed a case with the former Mixed Court. From then on, Tan Zhuo was no longer welcome in the family. However, this stimulated him to work hard. He was admitted to the Whampoa Military Academy in Guangdong and participated in several battles of the National Revolution, earning considerable merit. He retired from the army in 1930 and returned to Shanghai, deeply regretting his past impetuosity. He wanted to make amends for his past mistakes and repeatedly begged his father for forgiveness, so that he could return home and fulfill his filial duties. However, he was not allowed. He then filed a lawsuit with the former Shanghai Special District Court to confirm his parentage. After failing, he filed another lawsuit with the Shanghai First Special District Court to revoke the disownment declaration. However, it was ultimately rejected because it violated the principle of res judicata, as the essence of the two lawsuits was the same, although the relief sought was different. Now, Tan Zhuo, based on the Supreme Court's ruling No. 995 of 1934, argues that the parent-child relationship is natural and cannot be arbitrarily severed. Furthermore, there is no explicit provision in current law for parents and children to sever their relationship. Therefore, he, with the assistance of attorneys Chen Zhen and Liu Zhao, filed another lawsuit against his father, Tan Jingyu, with the Shanghai District Court, requesting the court to rule: (1) that the plaintiff has the right to inherit the defendant's property in the future; (2) that the defendant must not take any action that hinders the plaintiff's inheritance rights; and (3) that the defendant bears the litigation costs. The complaint states that the plaintiff is the defendant's son, which is not disputed by either party. Therefore, the plaintiff undoubtedly has the right to inherit the defendant's property under the law. Although the defendant has declared the disownment of his son, it does not have any impact on future inheritance. There would be no need to file a lawsuit to confirm this. However, because the defendant stated in the newspaper that he had severed the relationship with the plaintiff due to the plaintiff's improper behavior and had repeatedly refused the plaintiff's requests to return home and serve him, the plaintiff had to seek legal remedies. Subsequently, the court rejected the lawsuit based on the principle of res judicata. Since then, the defendant has repeatedly stated that the plaintiff is no longer his son and will not have any inheritance rights to his property in the future. It is clear that the defendant's intention to sever the relationship is to deprive the plaintiff of his inherent inheritance rights. However, according to the law, the parent-child relationship is natural and cannot be arbitrarily severed. There is no provision for disownment. Therefore, although the defendant has declared disownment, the parent-child relationship remains in effect in substantive law and does not affect the plaintiff's inheritance rights. However, since the defendant has expressed the intention to deprive the plaintiff of his inheritance rights and is already elderly, he must make arrangements for his property in advance. In the event of an accident, the plaintiff's siblings would naturally begin inheritance, and the plaintiff's rights would be in danger of being deprived before the confirmation is sought. It is necessary to request an immediate confirmation judgment. Therefore, the plaintiff requests the court to approve the requested items and make a judgment. Yesterday was the date scheduled for the trial. The defendant, Tan Jingyu, did not attend due to old age and was represented by attorney Hua Maosheng. The plaintiff, Tan Zhuo, appeared with his attorney, Chen Zhen, and explained the purpose of the lawsuit. The judge stated that it was inappropriate for fathers and sons to be involved in lawsuits and expressed a desire to persuade them to reconcile. However, since the defendant had not personally appeared, he instructed the defendant's attorney to inform the defendant that he must appear at the next hearing for persuasion in order to avoid litigation. The date for the next hearing will be notified later.

It is expected that enthusiastic individuals will actively participate to support the relief effort. The original letter from the company is transcribed below: "To whom it may concern, fellow countrymen are suffering from frequent natural disasters, causing immense grief. The company's colleagues are deeply saddened by this. We plan to hold a public competition of the company's famous chrysanthemums as they begin to bloom, to raise funds for the disaster victims. Since your association is a disaster relief organization, we hope you will support this charitable cause. We have drafted a plan and respectfully submit it for your consideration. If you agree, we will donate all proceeds to your association for distribution to the victims. Please reply as soon as possible so that we can proceed accordingly." Sincerely, the Xinxin Company. In addition, the fundraising group has sent a special letter to all representative banks, money shops, companies, and stores, requesting them to start collecting donations immediately. The letter includes the measures and hopes that all sectors will generously donate. The letter is transcribed below: "To whom it may concern, since the beginning of summer, there has been continuous rain, causing flooding in the Yangtze River and severe disaster in more than ten provinces, including Hubei, Shandong, Jiangxi, and Anhui. The situation is even worse than in 1931. Our association has appealed to all parties to raise funds to provide relief. However, this is a major undertaking that cannot be accomplished without collective effort. We are entrusting all banks, money shops, companies, and stores in the city to collect general donations for the flood. We have long admired your organization's enthusiasm for charity and concern for the hungry and destitute. We are sending you a copy of the donation collection measures, two posters, and various donation receipts (10 cents, 20 cents, 40 cents, 1 yuan, 2 yuan, 4 yuan, and 10 yuan) totaling a certain number of sheets. Please verify receipt and make efforts to solicit donations to support this good cause." Respectfully, the Fundraising Group of the Shanghai Flood Relief Association for Various Provinces. Measures for Entrusting All Banks, Money Shops, Companies, and Stores in the City to Collect General Donations for the Flood: (1) The Fundraising Group of the Shanghai Flood Relief Association for Various Provinces is entrusting all banks, money shops, companies, and stores to collect donations for the flood to facilitate donations from all sectors. (2) All banks, money shops, and stores must display posters about collecting donations for the flood in prominent locations to attract public attention. (3) All banks, money shops, and stores should report the daily collection of general donations to the temporary office of the fundraising group for publication in newspapers. (4) The period for collecting general donations by all banks, money shops, and stores is one month. (5) All banks, money shops, and stores should settle and submit the donations collected every half month to the temporary office of the fundraising group on the third floor of the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA for the association to report and announce in newspapers. (6) The general donation receipts collected by all banks, money shops, and stores are divided into seven types: 10 cents, 20 cents, 40 cents, 1 yuan, 2 yuan, 4 yuan, and 10 yuan. (7) All general donation receipts collected by all banks, money shops, and stores will be sent directly by the fundraising group of the association. After receiving all receipts, please fill out the return slip for verification. In addition, the association received 7,188 yuan from Mr. Shen Ailian et al., 6 yuan from Mr. Lin Kanghou's birthday celebration donation to disaster relief, old clothes and pants totaling 324 pieces collected by Miss Wenjie and a certain lady, 17 pairs of old shoes, 4 old quilts, and 3 old books and mirror frames.

Oilcake Producers Oppose Bran Tax. Shanghai Representatives Went to Shantou Yesterday to Negotiate. Gu Xinyi et al. Appeal to Huang Jilu for Assistance.

According to the Dagong News Agency, since Guangdong Province began levying bran tax on September 1, it has caused the oilcake and miscellaneous grain factories and transport merchants in various places to suspend operations. Although the manufacturers have repeatedly petitioned the central government's various ministries and commissions and telegraphed the Southwest Political Affairs Committee and the Finance Commissioner's Office of Guangdong Province, requesting its repeal, they have not received a satisfactory response, causing the industry to continue to suspend operations and transport. The standoff has lasted for nearly two months. Now, the factories in Shanghai, Kunshan, Wuxi, Changzhou, Hankou, and other places have jointly selected Gu Xinyi, Chen Ziyi, Jiang Hongbin, and others to explain the manufacturers' difficulties to Mr. Huang Jilu, a member of the Central Committee who came to Shanghai from northern Guangdong to attend the Sixth Plenary Session of the Central Committee (because Mr. Huang is a member of the Southwest Political Affairs Committee), and requested him to provide assistance in his personal capacity and find a way to revoke the tax order. In addition, they sent transport merchant representative Wu Zi to Shantou to negotiate with the local Miscellaneous Grain Association and other organizations to strive for the goal of abolishing the tax.

Customs General Affairs Department Announces: Regulations on Declaration Form Styles; Tong An Customs Brokerage Firm Penalized for Violations.

The General Affairs Department of the Jianghai Customs has issued two announcements regarding the penalty for violations by the Tong An Customs Brokerage Firm and the regulations on the style of customs declaration forms.

Violations and Penalties:

According to Article 18 of the Provisional Regulations for the Management of Customs Brokerages promulgated by the government on December 1, 1931, regardless of whether an individual, firm, or company has obtained a business license for a customs brokerage firm, if they act as a customs broker for others, once discovered, their firm name should be announced, and they will no longer be allowed to engage in such illegal business activities, and may be fined up to 5,000 yuan. Tong An has violated the aforementioned regulations and will be penalized. This is hereby announced for public knowledge.

Regulations on Style:

For import declarations of foreign goods, two copies of the manifest must be submitted to the customs, one printed in black and one printed in red, as announced in Bulletin No. 1467 on September 3, 1935. It is now stipulated that the copy printed in red should henceforth be printed entirely on red paper for the sake of distinction. As for the manifests with pure red printed lines that are still in stock, they can still be used as red inspection manifests. However, manifests printed with red lines and black characters or black lines and red characters must have a red stamp affixed to the right corner before the Customs can accept them. This stamp must be uniformly one inch wide and three inches long. All merchants are requested to take note of this. This is hereby announced for public knowledge.

The Ministry of Railways Formulates Settlement Notice for Material Purchase Payments; Orders the Two Railway Administrations to Comply.

The Two Railway Administrations received an order from the Ministry of Railways stating: "This Ministry has been ordering materials for various railways, and all related material prices are to be settled clearly by the respective railways before final clearance. Now, in order to facilitate the railways' clearance of material accounts and to easily understand the situation of material payments and debts, the Material Payment Management Committee of this Ministry has formulated a 'Settlement Notice for Material Purchase Payments' for each contract, which will be implemented from July 1 of this year. In the future, the railway administrations should directly settle accounts with the Committee in accordance with the method of material debt settlement specified in the Notice, in order to simplify the process." Enclosed with the order were five copies of the "Settlement Notice for Material Purchase Payments" format. The Bureau has instructed the Materials Department to comply.

To Address the Opium Problem, Managers of Various Hotels are Summoned for Instruction.

The Public Concession Police Department, noting the prevalence of hotels within the concession and the frequent use of these establishments as meeting places and hideouts for criminals, is concerned about the opium trade. It has been observed that opium addicts are setting up opium dens in hotel rooms, providing opium for others to smoke, which is deeply regrettable. Therefore, the authorities have scheduled a meeting at the Central Police Station on Sima Road at 2:00 PM on the 29th (today) to instruct the managers of various hotels. The managers are tasked with preventing guests from smoking opium within their premises and are required to report any suspicious individuals to the nearest police station via telephone. Failure to comply will result in the managers being held accountable. The Hotel Industry Association has been notified to inform all hotel managers to attend the meeting at the Central Police Station on time.
