Recent Situation of Long-Term Delivery in the Han Gang

Financial Circles Have Many Faults

Adjustment Feels Quite Difficult

Yesterday (the 18th) was only three days away from the end of the big competition in October. In general, a total conclusion must be made. In addition, the price of the delivery of a large number of securities in stock is quite huge. It is said that it is no less than ten million. From the surface, the total amount of income and expenditure can be resolved satisfactorily when it expires. However, from the content, the lack of remittance and allocation is often disparate. If it cannot be adjusted, it must rely on the assistance of powerful people. If a dealer with poor credit, it is not easy to get through the difficult period. It must do its best to seek employment in the market. For the sake of duty, yesterday’s foreign loan, although the surface was still 1.5 cents in the early morning, the allocation and water addition skyrocketed, and it rose to as high as 1.56 cents, and the situation still looked good. As for long-term delivery, yesterday’s amount due, the Qianzhuang side, was less than one million, and the bank side, was only several hundred thousand. Most of them were in transfer, and the interest rate was 8.5 yuan. Compared with the market price of 9.75 yuan for three or four types, it was also heard that the amount of long-term arrears due in Hankou was still more than six million in this session (all of which were amounts transferred from the previous "end of April"). It is difficult to clear this time, so it must be in the case of re-transfer. Its interest is more expensive than other industries. Yesterday, according to people in the industry, the long-term interest on transfers in Hankou was initially set at 11.5 yuan, and then increased by 50 cents to 1 yuan, which is the most expensive price of 12.5 yuan. Some Hankou Qianzhuang, which have long-term loans from Shanghai, cannot afford the high interest rates, and once requested a reduction, but most of them refused to reduce it. Therefore, there is a kind of solid Qianzhuang of Jiangsu and Zhejiang shareholders, which have all tried to raise funds to repay the loans. According to the investigation, about 700,000 to 800,000 loans have been repaid in this session. However, according to the overall observation, Hankou has been frequently plagued by disasters and market declines in recent years. I am afraid that it will not be able to raise such a huge amount of money.

The Seriousness of the Xianghe Incident

— Du

The Xianghe peasant revolt has become the focal point of national attention. County Magistrate Zhao Lianpu fled with the official seal to the Public Security Bureau, and the Director of the Public Security Bureau, Bai Zhichun, was brutally tortured by the rebel leader Wu Yiting. He issued orders and appointed administrative personnel within the county, and they went to obey. Liu Yaodong, a counselor from the provincial government, was dispatched to thoroughly investigate but was detained upon arrival. This situation shows Zhang's overbearing arrogance. Without external support, how could he be so rampant? The rumors spreading have caused much speculation in the Tianjin-Beijing area.

Examining the origins of the Xianghe Incident, it is said to stem from farmers resisting taxes. However, considering the current situation, it is far more significant than a small-scale riot. In this unfolding situation, we see countless figures behind the scenes pulling the strings. They are a group of people with no conscience. The so-called "farmers" may have been temporary puppets at the beginning, but soon they were discarded like autumn fans. Under the control of the bandits, with the participation of vagrants, can it truly be said that the farmers' intentions are being represented? The Sanhe Security Brigade had already entered the city once, so why was it suddenly withdrawn to its original defense? And the 32nd Army, which was sent to suppress the revolt, is still lingering outside the city, hesitating to exert pressure. How can they sit and watch Xianghe County become an extraordinary zone without taking active measures? Even if the Chinese army is incompetent, how can it be that they lack the ability to deal with even untrained farmers and dare not engage them in combat?

In this standoff of the Xianghe Incident, there are also rumors of unrest among the people of Sanhe County. Moreover, the counties along the war zone are being incited by Chinese traitors to respond to the revolt. The seriousness of its nature cannot tolerate further delay. For now, let us put aside all speculation and, based solely on the facts, seek an appropriate solution, feeling compelled to speak on three points. First, we believe that the Japanese side should promptly and clearly express its attitude. During this period of improved Sino-Japanese relations and the beginning of economic development, such an unfortunate incident will inevitably lead to unnecessary suspicions, posing an unexpected obstacle to mutual cooperation. Although the Japanese side vehemently denies any connection with the rebels, without concrete evidence, how can suspicions be dispelled? If Tada Hayao, after consulting with Shang Zhen, resolutely agrees to provide support and ceases using the war zone警戒綫 as an excuse to arbitrarily obstruct the advance of our troops, then the seeds of rebellion can be easily suppressed, and public doubts will naturally be resolved. Second, the people of the counties along the war zone should recognize the importance of national consciousness and seek to cultivate a stable and self-respecting character. Regardless of any dissatisfaction with the measures of the local government, they should not hastily believe the rumors spread by traitors or engage in reckless actions that would exacerbate the situation and alienate them from the rest of the nation. Third, the Hebei provincial authorities should handle this matter by seeking the understanding of the Japanese side through diplomatic channels while also making solid preparations for military suppression. They should adopt a resolute attitude and seek a swift resolution, avoiding hesitation or excessive consideration that would allow the situation to expand and become difficult to manage. According to yesterday's telegram, Shang Zhen had productive discussions with the Japanese side in Tianjin. Zhang Qingyu's security brigade has already entered Xianghe County and begun peaceful negotiations with the rebels. It seems that a solution is emerging. We sincerely hope for a smooth path forward without encountering unexpected setbacks.

League of Nations Transportation Committee Director Haas' Economic Report on China - Very Optimistic About the Future of China's Economic Construction - Advocates Centralized Management and the Establishment of Advisory Bodies - The Success of New China Lies in Restoring its Original Spirit

(Geneva) Dr. Haas, Director of the League of Nations Transportation Committee, was previously dispatched to China to investigate China's economic situation. After returning to Geneva, he drafted a report detailing his observations in China. The report, which has already been published, is approximately 22,000 words in length. In general, it expresses great optimism about the future of China's economic construction. He also deeply admired the spirit of the various Chinese technical experts who were immersed in their work and believed that the future of China's economic construction relied on such promising Chinese youth. He noted that this was often unknown to foreigners and highlighted it specifically. Dr. Haas believes that the most important aspect of China's economic construction is centralized management. The great success of sanitation work, for example, was due to this. Other tasks can be carried out in the same way. He suggests that several advisory bodies be established in the area of specialized technical consultation so that the relevant departments of the government can consult and decide at any time. The administrative power will still be in the hands of the various departments. In this way, the work of the National Economic Council can be reduced to facilitate its main work. Dr. Haas also expressed his admiration for the efforts of the authorities in various provinces for economic construction. He believed that the harmony of the Chinese nation and the deep-rooted national concept are a guarantee of a bright future. Although the circumstances in the various provinces and regions are different, the progress in construction is consistent, and public opinion is consistently behind the government. Therefore, the government can boldly implement its strategies. Young China is different from old China. It is very fond of work and not afraid of danger. Therefore, the future is very optimistic. Dr. Haas paid close attention to the importance of the rural economy and also said that the secret of the success of the New China lies in its ability to seek progress based on China's characteristics, rather than being eager for something new, but gradually restoring its original spirit. As for the central government's huge task, it is to connect the various provinces and use the lessons learned by the provinces in economic construction as a secret of success. As for the League of Nations' cooperation, it is only a small part of the work of the relevant departments. (Central News Agency, 28th)

Disaster Relief Funds for Guiding the Huai River Diverted to Urgent Relief in Pei County

(Xuzhou) The commissioner's office received a telegram from the province approving the allocation of 6,000 yuan for disaster relief travel expenses for Guiding the Huai River to be used for urgent relief in Pei County. Shao Hanyuan immediately withdrew the funds after receiving the telegram and sent Tian Suixiang to Pei County to hand them over to the disaster relief association for distribution. He also ordered Tian to be stationed in Pei County to assist in urgent relief matters. (Fuzhou) After political affairs, Chen Yi and his party left Taiwan for Fujian on the afternoon of the 28th. Chen will go to Beijing on the 3rd to represent the provincial army at the Fifth Plenary Session. Li Zeyi and Lin Zhiyuan will follow. (Special Dispatch, 28th)

Two Departments Revise the Method of Distributing Stamp Tax Fines

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Justice intend to revise the section of the "Provisional Regulations on Stamp Tax" and "Rules for Implementation" concerning the distribution of fines imposed by judicial organs. It is stipulated that in cases discovered by inspection agencies, 40% will be used for the operating expenses of judicial organs, 40% will be used for the operating expenses of inspection agencies, and 20% will be awarded to personnel who have made contributions to the matter. The two departments have now submitted the revisions to the Executive Yuan and the Judicial Yuan, which will forward them to the National Government for record. In addition, the Shanghai Municipal Government requested the Ministry of Finance to urge the Ministry of Justice to order the Shanghai Local Court to promptly allocate public expenses and bonuses for stamp tax violation cases sent by the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau for trial. The Ministry of Finance has forwarded the request and has also requested the Ministry of Justice to notify courts at all levels to handle and conclude stamp tax violation cases expeditiously and to allocate the fines collected expeditiously. (Central News Agency, 28th)
